           var tag = document.createElement('script');

tag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
var firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);

// 3. This function creates an <iframe> (and YouTube player)
//    after the API code downloads.
var player, lwcPlayer;
function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {

  if (document.getElementById('lwc-video')) {
    const youtubeId = document.getElementById('lwc-video').getAttribute('data-youtube-id');
    lwcPlayer = new YT.Player('lwc-video', {
        height: '315',
        width: '560',
        videoId: youtubeId,
        events: {
        'onReady': onPlayerReady,
        }
    });
  }
}

// 4. The API will call this function when the video player is ready.
function onPlayerReady(event) {
  if (document.getElementById('lwc-video')) {
    document.getElementById('lwc-video-thumbs').onclick = (e) => {
      document.getElementById('lwc-video-thumbs').style.display = "none";
      document.getElementById('lwc-iframe-wrapper').classList.add('active');
      lwcPlayer.playVideo();
    }
  }

}

  <!-- SUPPORT POPUP JS -->
  <script>
   var $ = jQuery.noConflict();

// 			function autoPlayVideo(vcode, width, height){
// 				"use strict";
// 				$("#video").html('<iframe width="'+width+'" height="'+height+'" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/'+vcode+'?autoplay=1&loop=1&mute=0&rel=0&wmode=transparent" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen wmode="Opaque"></iframe>');
// }

			// $('.video-thumbs > a').click(function(){
			// 	$('.video-thumbs').css({'visibility' : 'hidden', 'z-index' : '-5'});
			// 	autoPlayVideo('vUBLsWWbQSo','560','315');
			// })

	$('#popup-lead a.support-button').click(function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		$('#popup-lead').fadeOut('fast');
		$('#popup-lead #video').html('');
		setTimeout(function() {
			$('#donation-form').fadeIn();
		},500);
	});
	
	$('#donation-form #field_9_12, #donation-form #field_9_9, #donation-form .field--amount-choice, #donation-form .field--frequency, #donation-form #field_9_14').wrapAll('<div class="step-1"></div>');
	$('#donation-form #field_9_13, #donation-form #field_9_6, #donation-form #field_9_10, #donation-form #field_9_4, #donation-form #gform_9 .gform_footer').wrapAll('<div class="step-2"></div>');
	$('.campaign-form .field--amount, .campaign-form .field--amount-choice').wrapAll('<div class="flex-row"></div>');
	$('.campaign-form .field--email, .campaign-form .field--email-label').wrapAll('<div class="flex-row email-row"></div>');

	$('#next-button').click(function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		$('.step-1').fadeOut('fast');
		setTimeout(function() {
			$('.step-2').fadeIn();
		},500);
	});

			
    $("li.field--amount .gfield_radio > li").click(function() {
        var value = $(this)
            .find("input")
            .val();
		var total = value.substring(1, value.length);

        $(".field--amount-choice input").attr("value", total);
    });

    $(".field--amount-choice input").click(function() {
        $(".field--amount .gfield_radio > li > input").prop('checked', false);
    });

	$(document).ready(function() {
		var $ = jQuery.noConflict();
		
		// var isSupportPage = 0;
		
		// if ( isSupportPage ) return; 
		
		formConfirmation();
		
		// if( $('.support-popup-video').find('div.gform_confirmation_wrapper').length !== 0 ) {
		// 	$('.support-popup-video').addClass('form-submitted');
		// }

		// if( $('#donation-form').find('div.gform_validation_error').length !== 0) {
		// 	$('.support-popup-video').addClass('form-submitted');
		// }

		// if( $('#submitted-email').length !== 0 ) {
		// 	var email = $('#submitted-email').text();
		// 	console.log(email);
		// 	$('.field--email-followup .ginput_container_email input').val(email);
		// }
		
		
		var diff = 172800 * 1000; // 48 hours
		var showPopup = false;
		
		// 1. Get localStorage item for Popup to be shown
		const popup = document.querySelector('.general-popup');
		const lsItem = popup.hasAttribute('data-ls') ? popup.getAttribute('data-ls') : popup.id;
		
		if ( localStorage.getItem(lsItem) !== null ) {
			if ( localStorage.getItem(lsItem) === 'hideAlways' ) {
				showPopup = false;
			} else if ( Date.now() - localStorage.getItem(lsItem) < diff ) {
				showPopup = false;
			} else {
				showPopup = true;
			}
		} else {
			showPopup = true;
		}
		
		// 2. Bail out early if popup should not showe
		if ( showPopup === false ) return;
		
		$(window).load(function() {
			if ( showPopup === false ) return;
		});
		
		
		// 3. init popup on window scroll
		$(window).on("scroll", function(){
			if (showPopup === true ) {
				var scrollY = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
				var threshold = 1400;
				if ( scrollY > threshold && $('#support-popup').not(':visible') ) {
					if ( $('#support-popup').not(':visible') ) {
						setTimeout(function() {
							$('#support-popup').fadeIn();
							//  handleClose();
						}, 1000);
					}
				}
			} else {
				return;
			}
		});
		
		// Handle close (X) click
		$('.popup-close,.popup-close-link').click(function() {
			showPopup = false;
			closePopup();
		});
		
		// Handle click outside of popup
		$('.general-popup').click(function(event) { 
			var $target = $(event.target);
			if(!$target.closest('.popup-inner').length && $('.popup-inner').is(":visible")) {
				showPopup = false;
				closePopup();
			}        
		});
		
		let isSubscribed = false;
		
		// Check if Subscribe Form has been fulfilled
		jQuery(document).on('gform_confirmation_loaded', function(event, formId){
		    // Check if this confirmation is coming from Subscribe form
		   isSubscribed = popup.classList.contains('subscribe-popup') && popup.querySelector('.gform_confirmation_message_' + formId);
		   localStorage.setItem('subscribePopup', 'hideAlways');
		});
		
		
		function closePopup() {

			var stripeSuccess = getParameterByName('gf_stripe_success');
			if ( stripeSuccess !== null ) {
				// never show Donate Popup again
				// ls item name must match!
				localStorage.setItem('supportPop2', 'hideAlways');
			} else if (isSubscribed) {
				// never show Subscribe Popup again
				// ls item name must match!
				localStorage.setItem('subscribePopup', 'hideAlways');
			} else {
				localStorage.setItem(lsItem, Date.now());
			}
			
			showPopup = false;
			$('.general-popup').remove();

			// setTimeout(function() {
			// 	$('.general-popup').remove();
			// }, 1000);
		}

		function formConfirmation() {
			var stripeSuccess = getParameterByName('gf_stripe_success');
			if ( stripeSuccess !== null ) {
				// console.log('payment successful');
				$('.general-popup .popup-inner .text-column, .form-column > h3').hide();
				$('.gform_confirmation_wrapper.fundraising-form').closest('.form-column').addClass('confirmation');
			} 
		}
	});
  </script>
